$(document).ready(function(){

var $mainMenuItem = $('.first-level-' + i + '>a');

$dropdownContainer.insertAfter($mainMenuItem);
  
});

var $firstLevel = $('.et_mobile_menu .first-level > a');
var $allDropdowns = $('.et_mobile_menu [class*="dropdown-menu-container"]');

$firstLevel.off('click').click(function() {

$(this).attr('href', '#');  
var $thisDropdown = $(this).siblings(); 

$thisDropdown.slideToggle();
$(this).toggleClass('icon-switch');

var dropdownSiblings = $allDropdowns.not($thisDropdown);   
dropdownSiblings.slideUp();

var $thisFirstLevel = $(this);
var $firstLevelSiblings = $firstLevel.not($thisFirstLevel);
$firstLevelSiblings.removeClass('icon-switch');  

});

$(window).load(function() {

It aims to connect users with the best deals and promote <b>Regenerative Tourism</b> practices.</p></div></div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_1_tb_footer  et_pb_toggle_close"><h5 class="et_pb_toggle_title">What services does Miafrica offer?</h5><div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p>Miafrica offers a wide range of services, including:</p><ul><li><p><b>Travel Booking:</b> Tours, car rentals, resorts, hotels, and flights.</p></li><li><p><b>Customized &amp; Group Bookings:</b> Personalized itinerary planning and large-scale group booking services.</p></li><li><p><b>MICE Services:</b> Market research, event services, and booking for corporate meetings and events.</p></li><li><p><b>Work &amp; Study Abroad:</b> Guidance and opportunities for working or studying in destinations like the USA, Canada, and Dubai.</p></li><li><p><b>Regenerative Tourism:</b> Programs focused on sustainable travel that benefits local communities and ecosystems.</p></li></ul></div></div></div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_accordion et_pb_accordion_1_tb_footer et_animated"><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_2_tb_footer  et_pb_toggle_open"><h5 class="et_pb_toggle_title">What does MICE stand for, and what are your MICE services?</h5><div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p> <b>MICE</b> stands for <b>Meetings, Incentives, Conferences, and Exhibitions</b>. Miafrica’s MICE services include market research, event planning, and providing booking solutions and resources (<b>MICE Books</b>) specifically tailored for this corporate travel sector in Africa.</p></div></div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_3_tb_footer  et_pb_toggle_close"><h5 class="et_pb_toggle_title">Can Miafrica help me work or study abroad?</h5><div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p>Yes. Miafrica offers a <b>Work Abroad</b> service that provides information and opportunities for those looking to travel and work in countries like the USA, Canada, or Dubai. They also offer resources and application assistance for the <b>Study in Canada/US</b> program.</p></div></div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_4_tb_footer  et_pb_toggle_close"><h5 class="et_pb_toggle_title">What is Regenerative Tourism?</h5><div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p><b>Regenerative Tourism</b> is a model that goes beyond sustainability. It focuses on ensuring travel activities actively give back to local communities and ecosystems, leaving the destination better than it was found. Miafrica promotes and facilitates these types of travel experiences.</p></div></div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_5_tb_footer  et_pb_toggle_close"><h5 class="et_pb_toggle_title">Does Miafrica offer a travel business franchise opportunity?</h5><div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p>Yes. Miafrica promotes a <b>zero-cost startup</b> opportunity to launch your own African travel and tour business through their franchise program, allowing you to operate a home-based travel business.</p></div></div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_6_tb_footer  et_pb_toggle_close"><h5 class="et_pb_toggle_title">Are there training resources available?</h5><div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p>Yes, the platform provides <b>Travel Training</b> resources, including free certificates, through its online learning section to help individuals understand the travel industry.</p></div></div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_7_tb_footer  et_pb_toggle_close"><h5 class="et_pb_toggle_title">What are the other resources I can find on the website?</h5><div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p>Miafrica provides a variety of resources, including a <b>Travel Shop</b> for top-rated products, a <b>Blog</b> for travel insights and news, <b>Virtual Tours</b>, and information on <b>Top Travel Events in Africa</b>.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_1_tb_footer"><div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_1_tb_footer  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child"><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_1_tb_footer  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light"><div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2>Follow Us On</h2></div></div></div></div><div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_2_tb_footer et_pb_gutters1"><div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_6 et_pb_column_2_tb_footer  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough"><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_icon et_pb_icon_0_tb_footer">
